###########################################
### 	ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Events
###				  By Kolyn
###########################################

##Used for extra interaction with the rest of the galaxy. Primitives are not advised to attempt to reverse engineer or tamper its workings.

namespace = zofe_ascendancy_affairs

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Office
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = ascendancy_affairs_office_in_use
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
	}

	#Friendly Actions
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.friendly"
		custom_tooltip = zofe_ascendancy_friendly_action_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.10 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	#Mean Actions
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.mean"
		custom_tooltip = zofe_ascendancy_mean_action_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.20 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	#Internal
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.internal"
		custom_tooltip = zofe_ascendancy_internal_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1.exit"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = ascendancy_affairs_office_in_use }
				remove_global_flag = ascendancy_affairs_office_in_use
			}
		}			
	}
}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs (Friendly Action)

		}
	}

		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Menu (Energy Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.111
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.111.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.111.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {	
					ascendancy_sphere_of_influence = yes
					ascendancy_neighbors = yes
					ascendancy_subject_neighbors = yes
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.111.a"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }
		allow = { 
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = energy
				value >= 5000
			}
		}
		add_resource = { energy = -5000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1111 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.111.b"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_2 }

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1111
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1111.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1111.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = from
		planet_background = from
		graphical_culture = from
		city_level = from
		room = from
	}

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1111.a
		add_resource = { energy = 5000 }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			who = from
			modifier = opinion_gifted_us
		}
	}
}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Menu (Consumer Goods Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.113
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.113.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.113.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {	
					ascendancy_sphere_of_influence = yes
					ascendancy_neighbors = yes
					ascendancy_subject_neighbors = yes
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.113.a"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }
		allow = { 
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = consumer_goods
				value >= 5000
			}
		}
		add_resource = { consumer_goods = -5000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1131 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}

		hidden_effect = {

				has_technology = tech_fe_autonomous_fabricator

				has_technology = tech_omni_lance
				has_technology = tech_omni_emitter
				has_technology = tech_massive_autocannons
				has_technology = tech_omni_cannon
				has_technology = tech_omni_titan_lance
				has_technology = tech_fe_goliath
				has_technology = tech_lost_technologies_3
				has_technology = tech_paradise_creation
				has_technology = tech_paradise_creation_machine
				has_technology = tech_paradise_creation_hive
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.124 days = 0 }
		}
	}

			limit = {

					has_overlord = root

				}
				has_technology = tech_fe_class_5_singularity
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_dark_matter_power_plant

# ZoFE Ascendancy Action Menu (Agri-Processing Complex Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12413
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12413.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12413.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				country_uses_food = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				has_technology = tech_fe_gourmet_center
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_agri_processing_complex
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_agri_processing_complex
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

			exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1

# ZoFE Ascendancy Action Menu (Pico Forge Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12415
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12415.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12415.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				has_technology = tech_fe_nano_forge_2
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_pico_forge
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_pico_forge
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12415.a"
		trigger = { 
			exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_pico_forge
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_pico_forge
				}
			}
		}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Action Menu (Impossible Fortress Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12417
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12417.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12417.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				has_technology = tech_fe_aegis_complex_2
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_aegis_complex_3
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_aegis_complex_3
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12422.desc

		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root

			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_omni_lance
					has_tech_option = tech_omni_lance
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12422.a"
		trigger = { 
			exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_omni_lance
					has_tech_option = tech_omni_lance
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.92422 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12424
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12424.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12424.desc

	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_omni_cannon
					has_tech_option = tech_omni_cannon
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12424.a"
		trigger = { 
			exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_omni_cannon
					has_tech_option = tech_omni_cannon
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.92424 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Action Menu (Goliath Transfer Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1243
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1243.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1243.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_zofe_country = yes
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					has_overlord = root
					is_in_federation_with = root
				}
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_goliath
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_goliath
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1243.a"
		trigger = { 
			exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				NOR = {
					has_technology = tech_fe_goliath
					has_tech_option = tech_fe_goliath
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.12431 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}

			}

	diplomatic = yes

		portrait = from
		planet_background = from
		graphical_culture = from
		city_level = from
		room = from
	}

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2111.a
		event_target:AscendancyNabPopPlanet = {
			random_owned_pop = {
				limit = { is_same_species = root }
				kill_pop = yes
			}
		}
		from.capital_scope = {
			create_pop = { species = root }
		}
		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			who = from
			modifier = opinion_took_from_us
		}
	}

		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }
		allow = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				any_owned_leader = {
					leader_class = scientist
					has_skill > 4
				}
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				random_owned_leader = {
					limit = {
						leader_class = scientist
						has_skill > 4
					}
					save_event_target_as = AscendancyScientistTarget
				}
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2121 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2121
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2121.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2121.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = from
		planet_background = from
		graphical_culture = from
		city_level = from
		room = from
	}

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2121.a
		event_target:AscendancyScientistTarget = {
			unassign_leader = this
			set_owner = from
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			who = from
			modifier = opinion_took_from_us
		}
	}
}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Menu (Nab Fleet Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.213
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.213.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.213.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_overlord = root }
			every_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					#For Testing
					fleet_power > 50000
					any_controlled_ship = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military }
				}
				set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.213.a"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }
		allow = {
			NOR = {
				any_war = {
					any_attacker = { is_same_value = root }
					any_defender = { is_same_value = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1.owner }
				}
				any_war = {
					any_attacker = { is_same_value = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1.owner }
					any_defender = { is_same_value = root }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				save_event_target_as = AscendancyFleetTarget
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2131 }
				}
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.213.b"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_2 }
		allow = {

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.214
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.214.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.214.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_overlord = root
				any_neighbor_country = { is_same_value = root }
			}
			every_owned_fleet = {
				limit = { 
					is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
					solar_system = {
						any_neighbor_system = {
							exists = space_owner
							space_owner = { is_same_value = root }
						}
						any_system_planet = { is_colony = no }
					}
				}
				set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
			}
		}
	}

planet_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2211
	title = "colony.180.name"
	desc = "colony.180.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_asteroid_approaching_planet
	show_sound = event_air_raid_siren
	location = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		create_country = {
			name = "NAME_Incoming_Asteroid"
			type = faction
			auto_delete = yes
			flag = {
				icon = {
					category = "zoological"
					file = "flag_zoological_1.dds"
				}
				background= {
					category = "backgrounds"
					file = "new_dawn.dds"
				}
				colors={
					"black"
					"black"
					"null"
					"null"
				}
			}
			effect = {
				establish_communications_no_message = root.owner
			}
		}
		last_created_country = {
			set_country_flag = incoming_asteroid
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_Asteroid"
				effect = {
					set_aggro_range = 0
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_owner = PREV
					set_fleet_flag = asteroid_fleet
					save_event_target_as = asteroid_fleet_target
					create_ship = {
						name = "NAME_Asteroid"
						design = "NAME_Asteroid"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = ROOT
						distance = 75
						angle = random
					}
					queue_actions = {
						move_to = ROOT
						effect = {
							id = "colony.180.effect.10"
							ROOT = {
								planet_event = { id = colony.183 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_relation_flag = {
				who = root.owner
				flag = asteroid_enemy
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2221
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2221.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2221.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_dimensional_horror
	location = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2221.a
		hidden_effect = {
			solar_system = {
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = { is_star = yes }
					save_event_target_as = local_star
				}
				create_country = {
					name = "Dimensional Horror"
					type = faction
					auto_delete = yes
					flag = {
						icon= {
							category = "special"
							file = "extradimensional_02.dds"
						}
						background= {
							category = "backgrounds"
							file = "circle.dds"
						}
						colors={
							"black"
							"red"
							"null"
							"null"
						}
					}
					effect = {
						establish_communications_no_message = root.owner
						save_global_event_target_as = worm_invader
						create_fleet = {
							name = "YOUR WORLDS ARE MINE"
							settings = { spawn_debris = no }
							effect = {
								set_owner = event_target:worm_invader
								create_ship_design = {
									design = "NAME_Dimensional_Horror"
								}
								create_ship = {
									design = last_created_design
									name = "NAME_Worm-in-Waiting"
								}
								set_location = {
									target = event_target:local_star
									distance = 40
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2231
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2231.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2231.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_dimensional_horror
	location = ROOT
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2231.a
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_planet = {
				limit = { is_colony = yes }
				solar_system = {
					random_fleet_in_system = {
						limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase }
						create_ambient_object = {
							type = "psi_storm_1"
							location = prevprev
						}
						create_country = {
							name = "NAME_Psionic_Avatar_Country"
							type = faction
						}
						last_created_country = {
							set_country_flag = avatar_country
							create_fleet = {
								name = "NAME_Psionic_Avatar"
								settings = {
									can_upgrade = no
									can_change_composition = no
									can_change_leader = no
									uses_naval_capacity = no
									spawn_debris = no
									is_boss = yes
								}
								effect = {
									set_owner = PREV
									set_fleet_flag = avatar_fleet
									create_ship = {
										name = "NAME_Avatar"
										design = "NAME_Shroud_Avatar"
										prefix = no
										upgradable = no
									}
									set_location = last_created_ambient_object
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Menu (Punitive Sanctions Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.224
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.224.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.224.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				OR = {
					ascendancy_sphere_of_influence = yes
					ascendancy_neighbors = yes
					ascendancy_subject_neighbors = yes
					is_rival = root
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.224.a"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }
		allow = { 
			NOT = { has_modifier = punitive_sanctions }
			relative_power = {
				who = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1
				category = economy
				value >= superior
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2241 }
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes
		}
	}

		}

# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs Menu (Ruler Assassination Target)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.231
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.231.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.231.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root

		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes

					ascendancy_sphere_of_influence = yes

			is_at_war = no
			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = { exists = ruler }
		}

			event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 = {
				create_ruler_assassination_project = yes
			}
			ascendancy_affairs_office_available = yes

	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2311.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	show_sound = event_announcement
	location = root
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		fromfrom.owner = {
			ruler = {
				save_event_target_as = rulername
				kill_leader = {
					ruler = yes
					show_notification = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2311.a
		custom_tooltip = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.2311.a.tooltip
		fromfrom.owner = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				who = root.owner
				modifier = opinion_mean_to_us
			}
		}
	}
}




# ZoFE Ascendancy Affairs (Internal Affairs)
country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}

	#Starbase Redesign
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.redesign"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.31 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Ringworld Redesign
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.ringworld"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.32 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Space Debris Cleanup
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.debris"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.33 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Renounce Ascendancy
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.renounce"
		trigger = {
			zofe_sandbox = yes
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.34 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Rejuvenate Society
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.decadence"
		trigger = {
			zofe_sandbox = yes
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			is_gestalt = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Innervate Drones
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.decadence_hive"
		trigger = {
			zofe_sandbox = yes
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			has_authority = auth_hive_mind
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35 days = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	#Systems Check
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.30.decadence_machine"
		trigger = {
			zofe_sandbox = yes
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35 days = 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.10.exit"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.1 days = 0 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.31
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.31.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.31.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		planet_background = root
		graphical_culture = root
		city_level = root
		room = root
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clear_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		every_owned_fleet = {
			limit = {
				is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase
				OR = {
					is_ship_size = starbase_outpost
					is_ship_size = starbase_starport
					is_ship_size = starbase_starhold
					is_ship_size = starbase_starfortress
					is_ship_size = starbase_citadel
				}
				any_controlled_ship = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_spiritualist }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_spiritualist }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_spiritualist_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_spiritualist_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_materialist }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_materialist }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_materialist_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_materialist_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophile }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophile }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophobe }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophobe }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophobe_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_xenophobe_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_militarist }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_militarist }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_militarist_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_militarist_02 }
						}

							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_authoritarian }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_authoritarian }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_egalitarian_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_egalitarian_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_hive_mind }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_hive_mind }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_hive_mind_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_hive_mind_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_machine }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_machine }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = fallen_machine_02 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = fallen_machine_02 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = { graphical_culture = original_empire_01 }
							owner = { graphical_culture = original_empire_01 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_ascendancy_affairs_targets = yes
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = "zofe_ascendancy_affairs.31.a"
		trigger = { exists = event_target:ascendancy_affairs_target_1 }

		}

ship_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.311
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.311.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.311.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_federation_fleet
	show_sound = event_announcement
	location = root
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.311.a
		hidden_effect = {
			fromfrom = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_ship_size = starbase_citadel }
					destroy_fleet = this
					solar_system = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = "starbase_citadel"
							owner = root
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_ship_size = starbase_starfortress }
					destroy_fleet = this
					solar_system = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = "starbase_starfortress"
							owner = root
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_ship_size = starbase_starhold }
					destroy_fleet = this
					solar_system = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = "starbase_starhold"
							owner = root
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_ship_size = starbase_starport }
					destroy_fleet = this
					solar_system = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = "starbase_starport"
							owner = root
						}
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_ship_size = starbase_outpost }
					destroy_fleet = this
					solar_system = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = "starbase_outpost"
							owner = root
						}
					}	
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						is_planet_class = pc_utopian_ringworld

planet_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.321
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.321.name
	desc = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.321.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ringworld
	show_sound = event_construction
	location = root
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.321.a
		hidden_effect = {
			solar_system = {
				every_system_planet = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable
							is_planet_class =  pc_ringworld_seam 
							is_planet_class =  pc_ringworld_tech 
							is_planet_class = pc_utopian_ringworld
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							OR = {
								is_planet_class =  pc_ringworld_habitable
								is_planet_class = pc_utopian_ringworld
							}
						}
						set_planet_entity = {
							entity = "ringworld_habitable_entity_01_entity"
							graphical_culture = root
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							is_planet_class =  pc_ringworld_seam 
						}
						set_planet_entity = {
							entity = "ringworld_seam_entity_01_entity"
							graphical_culture = root
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							is_planet_class =  pc_ringworld_tech 
						}
						set_planet_entity = {
							entity = "ringworld_tech_entity_01_entity"
							graphical_culture = root
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35
	title = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35.name
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_gestalt = no }
		text = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35.desc
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_authority = auth_hive_mind }
		text = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35.desc.hive
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		text = zofe_ascendancy_affairs.35.desc.machine
